But when the second trip of the Spring Festival ended, I recalled that this hotel was not a particularly good memory.
When I drove from Shaoxing with my friends, I encountered rain and temperature drop and caught a cold. Both of us started to have a fever and were a little confused when we arrived at the hotel. When the car drove in, there was no obvious sign in the lobby. I drove around the hotel for at least 15 minutes (it should not be because my brain was confused, there was an Audi in front of me that was also looking for the lobby).
There were many people in the lobby, and there was a sense of assembly line when receiving customers. We told the front desk that we both had a fever. The only reply from the front desk was that we did not provide oral medicines and you bought takeout by yourself. There was no extra words, and continued to play with the phone and chat with colleagues.
Then I took a hot shower in the room and waited for the medicine to be delivered (drank a cup of Xiao Chaihu that I brought with me, and bought Gan Kang). Because the location was too remote, the takeout waited for an hour and then the front desk asked us to go to the front desk to pick it up before it was delivered.
After a nap, I didn't have the energy to get up just after 8 o'clock (I didn't oversleep and didn't have the energy to walk to the restaurant at the hotel entrance 500m away to eat), and unfortunately there was no food to eat. I can't understand why a resort hotel doesn't deliver food to the room, and the restaurant is still far away. The room is full of high-end books introducing the hotel's concept. In comparison, this most basic functional problem is very ironic. We were really hungry, hungry, and dizzy at the time, and felt like dying in the room.
We were in a small suite upstairs and downstairs, with only one quilt on the bed. I called back and said: You have to pay extra, this is a different price (playing a joke, but the reply is the same). Fortunately, the room itself is equipped with one, and we couldn't find it ourselves. Thank you for sending a gentle and kind auntie at the front desk to help us find a quilt to cover the quilt. Thank you for insisting on delivering the takeaway in the dark in the wind and rain to save my life. Although it was cold, at least we could fill our stomachs. I really miss the guy at the front desk who helped us remove the wrapping paper and put out a plate of heated bread at the Atour S where we stayed. ğŸ™ Thank you. Guantang, I'm sorry I was too delicate and couldn't go to a distant restaurant in the dark in the heat and rain to eat. I actually compared you with Atour.
Fortunately, it was just a cold. The next day, I was basically fully recovered. My friend also had no heat. Early in the morning, I took on the responsibility of finding food. I went to the lobby in the cold wind to call a car, wait for a car, and take a car to find (ask for) food. The signature yellow croaker noodles were gone, and the expected special cake was gone. I ate lonely, but at least I found some comfort in Wangzai milk. I nervously told the staff that my companion had a cold and wanted to take some porridge away. The other party threw two takeaway boxes and plastic bags to me before I finished listening to me. It took at least 20 minutes to pack the porridge and steamed buns and pickles in a hurry. I'm sorry that I'm clumsy and I'm not good at this. Then I couldn't find the battery car on the way back. I had just recovered from a cold and walked for 18 minutes to get to the room.            There is only one restaurant and it is far away, so it is inconvenient on rainy days.
Hygiene: clean and tidy
Environment: The park has a high greening rate, with rockeries, waterfalls and lotus ponds.
           The surrounding area is all farmland, factories, and villages.
Service: average
          The "Kaiyuan Guantang" garden series is more suitable for vacations. The front desk of "Yangming Guantang" in Yuyao is said to be three ancient buildings, but in addition to the living room and patio on the central axis, guest rooms are also built in the wings on both sides. The other guest rooms are small Chinese-style villas, each with three to five guest rooms.
    There is a large garden and rockery waterfall to the north, and there is COSTA coffee in the restaurant to the south. Opposite the restaurant is a large rice field and vegetable field. The old farmer who is harvesting celery said that the vegetable field can be used for restaurant tables and employee canteens. Instead, enjoy organic vegetables.
    The overall feeling is that Shaoxing's "Dayu Guantang" has a small commercial street compared to Yi, and next to it is the "Dayu Mausoleum".

name:Aâ€lâ€eâ€xâ€-â€Dâ€râ€eâ€aâ€m
info:Superior Garden View Twin Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Friends
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 8, 2023
msg:I knew about this newly opened Hui-style garden architecture hotel a few months ago. I entered the hotel gate on Friday night and went all the way to the lobby registration desk. Under the lighting effect, the white walls and black tiles of the Hui-style architecture, the reflection of the pool, the reflection of the lanterns, the quiet elegance, the magnificent momentum, I was really amazed.

The environment and architecture are beautiful. The boss designed them carefully. The three ancient buildings of Sixi Hall, Gengdu Hall, and Chengqing Hall are magnificent. It's like walking into a wealthy family in the Ming and Qing Dynasties. The gardens and courtyards of different sizes are also very beautiful. Because of the remote location, there is no need to worry about high-rise buildings coming into view. It happened to be autumn, and the garden was full of fruits. Persimmon trees, grapefruit trees, and pomegranate trees can be seen everywhere. The greening is very good. The small bridges and flowing water in the backyard, pavilions, and rockery waterfalls are completely designed according to the standards of Jiangnan gardens.

Overall, it is still a resort hotel worth staying in. It is suitable for all ages. The accommodation experience is very good and the breakfast is also good. There are many amusement facilities for children, so it is no problem to play all day. There are a lot of check-in activities, such as rice field train, concert, traditional games for National Day... You can also wear Hanfu to take pictures. Friends who like ancient buildings should not miss Mr. Fu's ancient building at 10 am every day. There is also an exhibition hall next to it, which has Wang Yangming and other Chinese and Japanese Confucian calligraphy exhibitions. There are also souvenirs for leaving the hotel.

But there are also disadvantages. There are more people on weekends, parent-child activities, and weddings. The hotel's parking spaces are not enough, and the roadside is full of cars all the way to the outside of the hotel, causing traffic jams. The hotel has no response measures. It is better to manage and open up suitable parking spaces.

The facilities in the room are very good, it is very comfortable to live in, the air conditioner is hot enough, and there is floor heating on the first floor, but the bathroom on the first floor smells like a sewer, maybe because it is rainy, it is recommended that the hotel put some air fresheners in the bathroom.
The staff are friendly and helpful. Xiao Wang was the one who received us. We are especially grateful to her. When I got home and found that I had forgotten something in the hotel, she even helped me find it and send it back. Thank you.

msg:Chinese-style garden hotel, just opened not long ago, very new environment and very good, the room does not have a particularly obvious smell, just from the point of view, it is still recommended;
If you want to eat, it is recommended not to eat in the hotel restaurant. We are too lazy to drive out, so dinner is settled in the hotel restaurant "Grannary", which can be said to be a negative score!
The chicken nuggets that came up first looked ok and were steaming, but they didnâ€™t taste hot at all. They were lukewarm. They were obviously leftovers for reprocessing, and there was no smell of chicken at all. I reported it to the waiter and took it again. When I went back, the chicken was still not hot when it was delivered, not to mention it was not fresh, I was so lazy that I didnâ€™t even want to return it to the oven;
Garlic pork ribs, barely edible, at least hot, the taste is the feeling of prepared dishes;
I didn't touch the pickled fish, and my friends said it was not delicious;
Stir-fried vegetables, the only delicious thing!
Brown sugar mochi, the taste is okay, but too oily!
More than 400 for 2 people, more than 200 per capita, this level is really bad, it is strongly recommended to avoid lightning!

msg:This is the first time I stayed in a hotel in the Guantang series. It is not so much a hotel, it is more like a tour of humanities and gardens in the south of the Yangtze River. The hotel has three ancient buildings. The decorations, furniture and plants here have a deeper understanding. It is the best and most profound explanation among all the ancient town explanations I have heard (according to observation, the explanation that day is the management staff who has a lot of affection for the hotel). It is worth recommending link
The scenery of the hotel is also very beautiful. Itâ€™s like being in Suzhou gardens. The service staff are very enthusiastic. They told us about the activities in the hotel on the day of check-in, and they would also say happy new year when they met. Because there is no elevator, the staff helped carry the luggage
We live in a double room, and our friends live in a twin room. I found that the double room is much smaller than the twin room, but the price is more expensive than the twin room, and the location is not as good as the twin room. The price/performance ratio is low
